Vocabulary

This vocabulary assumes all terms specified in the base Verifiable Credentials [[VC-DATA-MODEL]] context.

In addition, the following classes are available for specifying information related to supply-chain traceability.

You may view the latest json-ld vocabulary at:
https://w3id.org/traceability/v1

You may view the latest json-schema definitions at:
https://github.com/w3c-ccg/traceability-vocab/tree/main/docs/schemas

Undefined terms

This vocabulary uses '@vocab': 'https://w3id.org/traceability/#undefinedTerm' to disable JSON-LD related errors associated with Verifiable Credentials, issued about terms that have not yet been added here.

Agricultural Activity

An activity that takes place on the farm that needs to be recorded, such as planting, harvesting, applying fertilizer, etc.

Term AgActivity
Full IRI https://w3id.org/traceability#AgActivity
JSON Schema https://w3id.org/traceability/schemas/AgActivity.json

Farm

The Farm or business entity performing the activity.

Term farm
Full IRI https://w3id.org/traceability#dfn-entities

Actor

The actual person or persons performing the activity.

Term actor
Full IRI https://w3id.org/traceability#Person

Field

The field where the activity was performed.

Term field
Full IRI https://www.gs1.org/voc/Place

Activity Date

Date the activity occured.

Term activityDate
Full IRI https://schema.org/DateTime

Activity Type

Type of Avtivity, e.g. plant, harvest, spray.

Term activityType
Full IRI https://www.schema.org/value

Product List

Agricultural Product the Activity was performed on if known

Term agProduct
Full IRI https://schema.org/ItemList

Observation or Notes List

List of observations or notes related to the activity, such as spray mix, etc

Term observation
Full IRI https://w3id.org/traceability#observation

Agriculture Inspection Report

Information on the Inspection and the observations made

Term AgInspectionReport
Full IRI https://w3id.org/traceability#AgInspectionReport
JSON Schema https://w3id.org/traceability/schemas/AgInspectionReport.json

Facility

Information on the inspection facility.

Term facility
Full IRI https://www.gs1.org/voc/Place

Inspector

Inspector performing the Agriculture Inspection. The following link provides further insight: https://www.lawinsider.com/dictionary/food-inspector

Term inspector
Full IRI https://w3id.org/traceability#Inspector

Shipment

Details for a shipment of goods.

Term shipment
Full IRI https://schema.org/ParcelDelivery

Applicant

Entity that is applying for the inspection.

Term applicant
Full IRI https://w3id.org/traceability#dfn-entities

Inspection Date

Date of the completed inspection.

Term inspectionDate
Full IRI https://schema.org/DateTime

Inspection Type

Type of Inspection.

Term inspectionType
Full IRI https://www.schema.org/value

Observation List

List of observations as seen and specified in the Inspection Report schema, https://w3id.org/traceability#InspectionReport

Term observation
Full IRI https://w3id.org/traceability#observation

AgPackage

A package (container, crate, etc.) which holds agricultural products. The contents or the package itself should meet the requirements as specified here: https://www.producetraceability.org/documents/FINAL_PTI_Harmonized_Traceabilty_Case_Label_April_2020_(003).pdf

Term AgPackage
Full IRI https://w3id.org/traceability#AgPackage
JSON Schema https://w3id.org/traceability/schemas/AgPackage.json

Package Name

Name of the items within the package.

Term packageName
Full IRI https://schema.org/name

Food Grade

Grade of the agricultural products contained within the package. The following link contains more information on USDA food grading: https://www.ams.usda.gov/grades-standards

Term grade
Full IRI https://w3id.org/traceability#grade

Responsible Party

Entity that produced and packaged the products.

Term responsibleParty
Full IRI https://w3id.org/traceability#responsibleParty

Voice Pick Code

A four digit code digest of the GTIN code and Lot Code for use in integrating with voice picking systems. See the following PDF for more information: https://www.produceinventory.com/files/newsroom/Voice-Pick-Code.pdf

Term voicePickCode
Full IRI https://w3id.org/traceability#voicePickCode

Human readable date describing the date the package was packed, harvested, or is 'best by.'

Term date
Full IRI https://schema.org/DateTime

UPC Number

UPC (aka UPC-A) consists of 12 numeric digits that are uniquely assigned to each trade item. Along with the related EAN barcode, the UPC is the barcode mainly used for scanning of trade items at the point of sale, per GS1 specifications.

Term upc
Full IRI https://www.gs1.org/standards/barcodes/ean-upc

PLU Number

PLUs are a system of numbers that uniquely identify bulk produce sold in grocery stores and supermarkets. See the following link for further information: https://www.pma.com/content/articles/2014/05/plu-codes

Term plu
Full IRI https://w3id.org/traceability#plu

GTIN Code

Global Trade Item Number (GTIN) can be used by a company to uniquely identify all of its trade items.

Term gtin
Full IRI https://www.gs1.org/voc/gtin

Product

Product details as specified in the Product.json schema

Term product
Full IRI https://www.gs1.org/voc/Product

Scientific Name

The scientific classification of the agricultural product. Each plant has a scientific name comprised of a binomial which indicates the genus and specific identifier of the plant.

Term scientificName
Full IRI https://w3id.org/traceability#scientificName

Label Image URL

Image of the package label

Term labelImageUrl
Full IRI https://schema.org/url

Label Image Hash

Hash value for securely identifying the label image. More information can be found at the following link: https://cybersecurityglossary.com/hashing

Term labelImageHash
Full IRI https://w3id.org/traceability#labelImageHash

Bill Of Lading Number

This identifier might not be globally unique.

Term billOfLadingNumber
Full IRI https://schema.org/identifier

Booking Number

Reference number assigned by a carrier of its agent to identify a specific consignment such as a booking reference number when cargo space is reserved prior to loading.

Term bookingNumber
Full IRI https://service.unece.org/trade/uncefact/vocabulary/uncl1153/#Consignment_identifier_carrier_assigned

Purchase

Purchase documents related to a bill of lading

Term relatedDocuments
Full IRI https://schema.org/Purchase

SCAC

For maritime shipments, this code qualifies a Standard Alpha Carrier Code (SCAC) as issued by the United Stated National Motor Traffic Association Inc.

Term scac
Full IRI https://service.unece.org/trade/uncefact/vocabulary/uncl1153/#Standard_Carrier_Alpha_Code_(SCAC)_number

Carrier

The party providing the transport of goods in this consignment between named points.

Term carrier
Full IRI https://service.unece.org/trade/uncefact/vocabulary/uncefact/#carrierParty

Consignor

The party consigning goods, as stipulated in the transport contract by the party ordering transport.

Term consignor
Full IRI https://service.unece.org/trade/uncefact/vocabulary/uncefact/#consignorParty

Consignee

A party to which goods are consigned.

Term consignee
Full IRI https://service.unece.org/trade/uncefact/vocabulary/uncefact/#consigneeParty

Notify Party

The party to be notified upon arrival of goods and when special occurrences (usually pre-defined) take place during a transportation service.

Term notify
Full IRI https://service.unece.org/trade/uncefact/vocabulary/uncefact/#notifyParty

Freight Forwarder

The party combining individual smaller consignments into a single larger shipment (the consolidated shipment), which is sent to a counterpart that mirrors the consolidator's activity by dividing the consolidated consignment into its original components.

Term freightForwarder
Full IRI https://service.unece.org/trade/uncefact/vocabulary/uncefact/#freightForwarderParty

Freight

Content described by the bill of lading

Term freight
Full IRI https://schema.org/ParcelDelivery

NMFC Freight Class

The National Motor Freight Classification® (NMFC®) is a standard that allows for determining of freight classes for the comparison of different commodities and products being shipped.

Term nmfcFreightClass
Full IRI https://w3id.org/traceability#nmfcFreightClass

Hazard Code

The Department of Transportation (DOT) hazard code associated with the shipment.

Term hazardCode
Full IRI https://w3id.org/traceability#hazardCode

Port of Loading

The first arrival location in a transport. This would be a port for sea, an airport for air, a terminal for rail, or a border post for land crossing.

Term placeOfIssue
Full IRI https://service.unece.org/trade/uncefact/vocabulary/uncl3227/#Place_of_loading

Port of Discharge

The final exporting location in a transport. This would be a port for sea, an airport for air, a terminal for rail, or a border post for land crossing.

Term placeOfIssue
Full IRI https://service.unece.org/trade/uncefact/vocabulary/uncl3227/#Place_of_discharge

Formula

A chemical formula is a way of presenting information about the chemical proportions of atoms that constitute a particular chemical compound or molecule, using chemical element symbols, numbers, and sometimes also other symbols, such as parentheses, dashes, brackets, commas and plus and minus signs.

Term formula
Full IRI https://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/chebi/formula

InChI

The IUPAC International Chemical Identifier (InChI) is a textual identifier for chemical substances, designed to provide a standard way to encode molecular information and to facilitate the search for such information in databases and on the web.

Term inchi
Full IRI https://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/chebi/inchi

InChIKey

The condensed, 27 character InChIKey is a hashed version of the full InChI (using the SHA-256 algorithm), designed to allow for easy web searches of chemical compounds.

Term inchikey
Full IRI https://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/chebi/inchikey

DCSA Shipping Instruction

The Shipping Instruction is an enrichment to the original booking shared by the shipper to the carrier. The shipping instruction includes volume or weight, cargo items, shipping dates, origin, destination, and other special instructions. The information given by the shipper through the shipping instruction is the information required to create a Transport Document. Based on DCSA's eBL specification (https://dcsa.org/standards/ebill-of-lading)

Term DCSAShippingInstruction
Full IRI https://service.unece.org/trade/uncefact/vocabulary/uncefact/#Instructions
JSON Schema https://w3id.org/traceability/schemas/DCSAShippingInstruction.json

DCSA Transport Document

The document that governs the terms of carriage between shipper and carrier for maritime transportation. Two distinct types of transport documents exist: Bill of Lading, Sea Waybill. Based on DCSA's eBL specification (https://dcsa.org/standards/ebill-of-lading)

Term DCSATransportDocument
Full IRI https://api.swaggerhub.com/domains/dcsaorg/DCSA_DOMAIN/1.0.1#/components/schemas/transportDocument
JSON Schema https://w3id.org/traceability/schemas/DCSATransportDocument.json

Shipping Instruction

The Shipping Instruction is an enrichment to the original booking shared by the shipper to the carrier. The shipping instruction includes volume or weight, cargo items, shipping dates, origin, destination, and other special instructions. The information given by the shipper through the shipping instruction is the information required to create a Transport Document.

Term shippingInstruction
Full IRI https://api.swaggerhub.com/domains/dcsaorg/DCSA_DOMAIN/1.0.1#/components/schemas/shippingInstruction

IntentToSell

A simple case where an entity (person or organization) wishes to notify some third party that they intend to sell some product, likely into a different geographic region than in originated in. This is a highly simplified version of an LOI that can be used to identify and declare intent earlier in the process than would be possible otherwise. This object may be easily subclassed for extension with other data for other cases where additional regulatory data may be required

Term IntentToSell
Full IRI https://w3id.org/traceability#IntentToSell
JSON Schema https://w3id.org/traceability/schemas/IntentToSell.json

Measurement Value

A floating-point numeric value that is qualified by the corresponding measurement unit code - see gs1:unitCode.

Term value
Full IRI https://www.schema.org/value

Measurement Unit

A string value indicating a Measurement Unit from UN/ECE Recommendation 20, Units of Measure used in International Trade, e.g., GRM = gram - see rec20_rev3

Term unitCode
Full IRI https://schema.org/unitCode

Mechanical Property

A property, used to indicate attributes and relationships of some Thing; equivalent to rdf:Property.

Term MechanicalProperty
Full IRI https://w3id.org/traceability#MechanicalProperty
JSON Schema https://w3id.org/traceability/schemas/MechanicalProperty.json

Phytosanitary

Generalized schema capture of most common phytosanitary inspection data and properties. Any phyto forms that deviate greatly from this will need their own schemas, unless it seems like the properties are more universal and should be added to this schema.

Term Phytosanitary
Full IRI https://w3id.org/traceability/Phytosanitary
JSON Schema https://w3id.org/traceability/schemas/Phytosanitary.json

Certificate Number

ID number of the certificate

Term certificateNumber
Full IRI https://schema.org/identifier

Plant Protection Organization

The phytosanitary standard-setting organization for a region.

Term plantOrg
Full IRI https://www.gs1.org/voc/Organization

Distinguishing Marks

Any notable marks or variants of the items being inspected.

Term distinguishingMarks
Full IRI https://www.gs1.org/voc/variantDescription

Port of Entry

US port through which the imports passed. Click the following link for more information: https://www.govinfo.gov/content/pkg/CFR-2011-title19-vol1/pdf/CFR-2011-title19-vol1-sec24-24.pdf

Term portOfEntry
Full IRI https://w3id.org/traceability#portOfEntry

Additional Declaration

Additional declaration for the plants being shipped and inspected.

Term additionalDeclaration
Full IRI https://schema.org/Comment

Inspection Notes

Any notes or comments the inspector wishes to make relevant to the inspection.

Term notes
Full IRI https://schema.org/Comment

Disinfection Date

Date when the disinfection treatment was applied.

Term disinfectionDate
Full IRI https://schema.org/validFrom

Disinfection Treatment

Type of disinfection treatment applied to the product. More information can be found at the following link: https://www.ecfr.gov/cgi-bin/text-idx?rgn=div5&node=7:5.1.1.1.4#se7.5.305_12

Term disinfectionTreatment
Full IRI https://w3id.org/traceability#disinfectionTreatment

Disinfection Chemical

Chemical and/or active ingredient used in the disinfection.

Term disinfectionChemical
Full IRI https://schema.org/activeIngredient

Disinfection Duration

Duraction that the disinfection chemical was applied.

Term disinfectionDuration
Full IRI https://schema.org/duration

Disinfection Temperature

Temperature at which the disinfection chemical was applied.

Term disinfectionTemperature
Full IRI https://schema.org/MeasuredValue

Disinfection Concentration

Chemical concentration at which the disinfection chemical was applied in the disinfection process. More information can be found at the following link: https://chem.libretexts.org/Bookshelves/General_Chemistry/Map%3A_Chemistry_-_The_Central_Science_(Brown_et_al.)/04._Reactions_in_Aqueous_Solution/4.5%3A_Concentration_of_Solutions

Term disinfectionConcentration
Full IRI https://w3id.org/traceability#disinfectionConcentration

signatureDate

Date when the inspection was signed by the inspection officer.

Term signatureDate
Full IRI https://schema.org/DateTime

Inspection Date

Date of the completed inspection.

Term inspectionDate
Full IRI https://schema.org/DateTime

Facility

Information on the inspection facility.

Term facility
Full IRI https://www.gs1.org/voc/Place

Inspector

Inspector performing the Agriculture Inspection. More information can be found at the following link: https://www.lawinsider.com/dictionary/food-inspector

Term inspector
Full IRI https://w3id.org/traceability#Inspector

Shipment

Details for a shipment of goods.

Term shipment
Full IRI https://schema.org/AgParcelDelivery

Agriculture Package

Package, crate, or other container holding an agricultural product or products for inspection.

Term agPackage
Full IRI https://w3id.org/traceability#AgPackage

Applicant

Entity that is applying for the inspection.

Term applicant
Full IRI https://w3c-ccg.github.io/traceability-vocab/#dfn-entities

Inspection Type

Type of Inspection.

Term inspectionType
Full IRI https://www.schema.org/value

Observation List

List of observations

Term observation
Full IRI https://schema.org/ItemList

Place

Entities that have a somewhat fixed, physical location.

Term Place
Full IRI https://schema.org/Place
JSON Schema https://w3id.org/traceability/schemas/Place.json

Global Location Number (GLN)

A Global Location Number (GLN) is the GS1 Identification Key used to identify physical locations or parties. The key comprises a GS1 Company Prefix, Location Reference and Check Digit. For more information, see http://www.gs1.org/gln.

Term globalLocationNumber
Full IRI https://schema.org/globalLocationNumber

Geographic Coordinates

Links to information about geocoordinates for a place.

Term geo
Full IRI https://schema.org/GeoCoordinates

Postal Address

The postal address for an organization or place.

Term address
Full IRI https://schema.org/PostalAddress

UN Locode

LOCODE

Term unLocode
Full IRI https://service.unece.org/trade/uncefact/vocabulary/uncefact/#UNECELOCODE

Postal Address

The location at which a particular organization or person may be found or reached.

Term PostalAddress
Full IRI https://schema.org/PostalAddress
JSON Schema https://w3id.org/traceability/schemas/PostalAddress.json

Organization Name

The name of the organization expressed in text.

Term organizationName
Full IRI https://gs1.org/voc/organizationName

Street Address

The street address expressed as free form text. The street address is printed on paper as the first lines below the name. For example, the name of the street and the number in the street or the name of a building.

Term streetAddress
Full IRI https://schema.org/streetAddress

Address Locality

Text specifying the name of the locality; for example, a city.

Term addressLocality
Full IRI https://schema.org/addressLocality

Address Region

Text specifying a province or state in abbreviated format; for example, NJ.

Term addressRegion
Full IRI https://schema.org/addressRegion

Address Country

Code specifying the country (and country subdivision) for the address using ISO 3166-1.

Term addressCountry
Full IRI https://schema.org/addressCountry

Cross Street

A street intersecting a main street (usually at right angles) and continuing on both sides of it.

Term crossStreet
Full IRI https://gs1.org/voc/crossStreet

County Code

A code that identifies a county. A county is a territorial division in some countries, forming the chief unit of local administration. In the US, a county is a political and administrative division of a state.

Term countyCode
Full IRI https://gs1.org/voc/countyCode

Postal Code

Text specifying the postal code for an address.

Term postalCode
Full IRI https://schema.org/postalCode

Post Office Box Number

The number that identifies a PO box. A PO box is a box in a post office or other postal service location assigned to an organization where postal items may be kept.

Term postOfficeBoxNumber
Full IRI https://schema.org/postOfficeBoxNumber

PriceSpecification

A structured value representing a price or price range.

Term PriceSpecification
Full IRI https://schema.org/PriceSpecification
JSON Schema https://w3id.org/traceability/schemas/PriceSpecification.json

Example Verifiable Credential

    {
  "id": "http://example.org/credentials/",
  "type": [
    "VerifiableCredential"

Equipment Reference

The unique identifier for the equipment, which should follow the BIC ISO Container Identification Number where possible. According to ISO 6346, a container identification code consists of a 4-letter prefix and a 7-digit number (composed of a 3-letter owner code, a category identifier, a serial number, and a check-digit). If a container does not comply with ISO 6346, it is suggested to follow Recommendation #2 “Container with non-ISO identification” from SMDG.

Term equipmentReference
Full IRI https://service.unece.org/trade/uncefact/vocabulary/uncefact/#identificationId

ISO Equipment Code

Unique code for the different equipment size/type used for transporting commodities. The code is a concatenation of ISO Equipment Size Code and ISO Equipment Type Code A and follows the ISO 6346 standard.

Term ISOEquipmentCode
Full IRI https://api.swaggerhub.com/domains/dcsaorg/DCSA_DOMAIN/1.0.1#/components/schemas/ISOEquipmentCode

USMCA Certificate Of Origin

The new United States-Mexico-Canada Agreement (USMCA) allows importers to complete a certification of origin to include nine required data elements as well as a certification statement. These data elements do not need to follow a prescribed format. The USMCA also allows a certification of origin to be completed and signed with an electronic or digital signature.

Term USMCACertificateOfOrigin
Full IRI https://w3id.org/traceability#USMCACertificateOfOrigin
JSON Schema https://w3id.org/traceability/schemas/USMCACertificateOfOrigin.json

No example VC for USMCACertificateOfOrigin

Certifier

Importer, Exporter, or Producer Certification of Origin: Indicate whether the certifier is the exporter, producer, or importer in accordance with Chapter 5, Article 5.2 (Claims for Preferential Tariff Treatment) of the agreement.

Term importer
Full IRI https://w3id.org/traceability#certifier

Exporter's Details

Exporter’s name, address (including country), email address, and telephone number, if different than the certifier. This information is not required if the producer is completing the Certification of Origin and does not know the identity of the exporter. The address of the exporter shall be the place of export of the good in a Party’s territory.

Term exporterDetails
Full IRI https://w3id.org/traceability#exporterDetails

Producer's Details

Producer’s name, address (including country), email address, and telephone number, if different than the certifier or exporter, or, if there are multiple producers, state 'Various' or provide a list of producers. A person that wants this information to remain confidential may state 'Available upon request by the importing authorities.' The address of a producer shall be the place of production of the good in a Party's territory.

Term producerDetails
Full IRI https://schema.org/manufacturer

Producer Confidential

A person that wants the producer information to remain confidential may state 'Available upon request by the importing authorities.'

Term exporterDetails
Full IRI https://w3id.org/traceability#producerConfidential

Importer's Details

Importer’s name, address, email address, and telephone number (if known). The address of the importer shall be in a Party's territory. If the identity of the importer is unknown, or there are various importers, please check the appropriate box.

Term importerDetails
Full IRI https://w3id.org/traceability#importerDetails

Importer Unknown

If the identity of the importer is unknown, or there are various importers, please check the appropriate box.

Term exporterDetails
Full IRI https://w3id.org/traceability#importerUnknown

Origin Criterion

Specify the Origin Criterion under which the good qualifies, as set out in Chapter 4, Article 4.2 (Originating Goods) of the USMCA/T-MEC/CUSMA agreement (https://ustr.gov/sites/default/files/files/agreements/FTA/USMCA/Text/04-Rules-of-Origin.pdf). Criterion A: The good is wholly obtained or produced entirely in the territory of one or more of the USMCA/T-MEC/CUSMA countries, as defined in Article 4.3 of the Agreement; Criterion B: The good is produced entirely in the territory of one or more of the USMCA/T-MEC/CUSMA countries using non-originating materials, provided the good satisfies all applicable requirements of product-specific rules of origin; Criterion C: The good is produced entirely in the territory of one or more of the USMCA/T-MEC/CUSMA countries exclusively from originating materials; or Criterion D: The good is produced entirely in the territory of one or more of the USMCA/T-MEC/CUSMA countries. It is classified with its materials, or satisfies the 'unassembled goods' requirement, and meets a regional value content threshold of not less than 60% if the transaction value method is used, or not less than 50% if the net cost method is used (not including RVC for autos); except for goods in Chapter 61-63 of the HTS.

Term importer
Full IRI https://w3id.org/traceability#originCriterion
